The staff members were incredibly attentive and friendly, always ready to assist with any inquiries or requests. However, one minor inconvenience was the lack of a handle on the window in my room. While this didn't detract significantly from my stay, it would have been more convenient not to have to call for assistance each time I wanted to open the window for some fresh air.

Despite this small issue, I thoroughly enjoyed my time at the Castle Hotel. The amenities were top-notch, the dining options were exquisite, and the location was perfect for exploring the surrounding area. I would highly recommend this hotel to anyone looking for a memorable and luxurious stay.

I spent almost 2 hours of my vacation trying to get a suitable response which was really annoying. This sort of 5 star accommodation should provide much better service. Finally after much complaining falling on deaf ears we were offered a different room with the same heating issue plus a bottle of red wine which seemed particularly absurd considering we still had 3 nights to stay at it is the middle of winter! We decided that we did not want to waste any more time complaining about something nobody knew how to fix so we remained in our original room and kept the window slightly open. 
 In my opinion this is totally unacceptable and a hotel of this standard should have staff in house that ensure that crucial hotel infrastructure is working well at all times during all seasons. 
 While the hotel did gift us wine and attempted to provide a solution we felt totally let down and it did affect our room comfort. Furthermore offering us only 2 nights refund after staying one night and complaining is not good enough. In future we will probably select the Hyatt instead!

name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Deluxe Mountain-view Twin Room
info:Stayed in October 2023
info:Family
info:2 Reviews
rating:4.2
posted:Posted October 9, 2023
msg:1. Overview
The old mother had always wanted to visit Dalian, but it happened to be rainy in Pingshan Grand Canyon and Jiuzhaigou Scenic Area during the National Day, so she changed her route to Dalian, Shenyang. Dalian Yifang Castle Hotel is unique in the appearance of the building and is highly recognizable. I have always wanted to experience it, and this time I got my wish.
1. Membership level: Platinum
2. Book a room type: Twin room with mountain view
3. Upgraded room type: Twin room with sea view
4.Member benefits: double breakfast, no executive lounge
Before coming here, I read many experience reports on Yifang Castle, with mixed reviews and mixed reviews. In a practical and realistic manner, I would like to share with you my true experience of staying here.
2. Check-in
Yifang Castle is located halfway up the mountain. It is about 500 meters from the road down the mountain to the hotel lobby. You can take a taxi directly to the hotel lobby, you can walk to the lobby, or you can contact the hotel concierge to arrange a free shuttle bus inside the gate (Picture 7) Waiting for pickup.
You will be asked to pay a deposit of 1,000 yuan during check-in, which will be returned the same way after check-out. It still feels quite cumbersome. Most hotels no longer adopt this method. The Platinum Card souvenir includes a box of homemade mochi and two snack coupons (Picture 10). The snack coupons can be chosen from castle-shaped sorbet (Picture 11), two cups of coffee, a cup of juice, and one of homemade macarons. There is no welcome fruit, but a small dessert (Picture 8) instead.
When I checked in at noon on October 6th, the attitude of the red-shirted service staff was particularly good, and the shuttle bus driver was also very dedicated. The attitude of other service staff was relatively average.
3. Guest rooms
The booked mountain view twin room and the upgraded sea view twin room are both 60 square meters. The bathroom has double wash basins, dry and wet are separated, and the supplies have been replaced by large bottles. The bedding in the bedroom is generally comfortable, but there is no main light, which is a bit unfamiliar. Tables, chairs, cabinets, and curtains are not well maintained and have old dirt (Figure 14). In line with the principle of keeping out of sight, we narrow our sight distance and no longer look closely. Looking out the window is the Xinghai Bridge (Picture 6). The scenery is really good, and I have to say that the location is excellent.
4. Catering
Except for breakfast in the hotel, everything was eaten outside. Breakfast started at 6:30. We went to the restaurant early in the morning to catch our flight. The restaurant is not big, but the variety of food is okay, especially the carbohydrates.
5. Facilities
Basically no experience.
6. Precautions
1. The hotel is a 20-minute drive from Zhoushuizi Airport. However, it is not easy to call online taxis before 8 o'clock in the morning. If you need it, you can consider taking a taxi in advance. It's very close to Xinghai Square, so you can take a stroll there after dinner.
2. The hotel shuttle bus service time ends at 9:50 p.m.
3. Drones are not allowed to fly inside the hotel. If necessary, they can take off outside the hotel. It is recommended to keep a little distance to avoid affecting the rest and daily life of others. Due to the tight schedule, I only took a few pictures.
7. Overall evaluation
Expected, unexpected. There is a big difference between reading other people's reviews and personal experience. Yifang Castle is still worth checking in and experiencing, at least it has been well received by my old mother.

Adjacent to Xinghai Square, the largest city square in Asia
It can be called the landmark building of Dalian.

If you must put a label on this hotel

Whether it is the appearance of the hotel, the view of the room, or the sky garden

Not many people check in
